- Title: An executive resolution authorizing the en bloc consideration in Executive Session of certain nominations on the Executive Calendar.
- Congress: 119
- Bill type: SRES
- Bill number: 377
- Origin chamber: Senate
- Introduced date: 2025-09-08
- Update date: 2026-03-12T15:09:01Z

## Timeline

- 2025-09-08: Introduced in Senate
- 2025-09-08 - IntroReferral: Introduced in Senate
- 2025-09-08 - Calendars: Placed on Senate Executive Calendar under Over, Under the Rule. Calendar No. 1.
- 2025-09-08 - IntroReferral: Submitted in the Senate. Placed on Senate Executive Calendar under Over, Under the Rule.
- 2025-09-09 - Floor: Cloture motion on the measure presented in Senate. (CR S6462)
- 2025-09-09 - Floor: Measure laid before Senate by motion. (consideration: CR S6461)
- 2025-09-09 - Floor: Motion to proceed to executive session to consideration of measure agreed to in Senate by Yea-Nay Vote. 53 - 45. Record Vote Number: 511.
  - Recorded vote: Senate session 1, roll 511 (2025-09-09T23:36:06Z)
- 2025-09-09 - Floor: Motion to table the point of order made by Senator Schumer, the question being: Is a resolution for the en bloc consideration of specific nominations on the Executive Calendar required to be considered in legislative session? agreed to in Senate by Yea-Nay Vote. 53 - 46. Record Vote Number: 510.
  - Recorded vote: Senate session 1, roll 510 (2025-09-09T22:28:38Z)
- 2025-09-09 - Floor: Point of order by Senator Schumer that the motion to proceed to Executive Session to consider Executive Calendar No. 1, S.Res. 377, is not in order because legislation that provides for the en bloc consideration of individual nominations is legislative business and should be considered in legislative session raised in Senate.
- 2025-09-09 - Floor: The Chair, under the provisions of Rule XX, submits the question to the Senate for its decision: Is a resolution for the en bloc consideration of specific nominations on the Executive Calendar required to be considered in legislative session?.
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: By unanimous consent agreement, mandatory quorum required under Rule XXII waived.
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: Cloture not invoked in Senate by Yea-Nay Vote. 52 - 47. Record Vote Number: 513. (CR S6564-6565)
  - Recorded vote: Senate session 1, roll 513 (2025-09-11T19:46:20Z)
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: Motion by Senator Thune to appeal the ruling of the chair that the threshold for cloture on an Executive resolution for en bloc consideration of nominations with a calendar number on the Executive Calendar, other than those on level 1 of the Executive Schedule under 5 U.S.C. 5312 or.
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: Motion by Senator Thune to reconsider the vote by which cloture on S. Res. 377 was not invoked (Record Vote No. 513) agreed to in Senate by Yea-Nay Vote. 52 - 45. Record Vote Number: 514.
  - Recorded vote: Senate session 1, roll 513 (2025-09-11T20:52:26Z)
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: Motion by Senator Thune to reconsider the vote by which cloture on S. Res. 377 was not invoked (Record Vote No. 513) made in Senate.
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: Point of order by Senator Thune that consistent with the precedent of the Senate on November 21, 2013, the threshold for cloture on an Executive resolution for en bloc consideration of nominations with a calendar number on the Executive Calendar, other than those on Level 1 of the Executive Schedule under 5 U.S.C. 5312, or Article 3 judges, is a simple majority raised in Senate.
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: Ruling of the Chair that the point of order raised by Senator Thune with respect to the precedent set on November 21, 2013 regarding the threshold for cloture on an Executive resolution for en bloc consideration of nominations with a calendar number on the Executive Calendar, other than those on level 1 of the Executive Schedule under 5 U.S.C. 5312, or Article 3 judges not sustained by Yea-Nay Vote. 45 - 53. Record Vote Number: 515.
  - Recorded vote: Senate session 1, roll 515 (2025-09-11T21:08:06Z)
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: Ruling of the Chair that the point of order raised by Senator Thune with respect to the precedent set on November 21, 2013 regarding the threshold for cloture on an Executive resolution for en bloc consideration of nominations with a calendar number on the Executive Calendar, other than those on level 1 of the Executive Schedule under 5 U.S.C. 5312, or Article 3 judges, ruled out of order.
- 2025-09-11 - Floor: Upon reconsideration, cloture on the measure invoked in Senate by Yea-Nay Vote. 53 - 43. Record Vote Number: 516. (CR S6564)
  - Recorded vote: Senate session 1, roll 516 (2025-09-11T21:31:28Z)
- 2025-09-15 - Floor: Considered by Senate. (consideration: CR S6591)
- 2025-09-15 - Floor: Passed/agreed to in Senate: Resolution agreed to in Senate without amendment by Yea-Nay Vote. 51 - 44. Record Vote Number: 517.
  - Recorded vote: Senate session 1, roll 517 (2025-09-15T22:14:53Z)
- 2025-09-15 - Floor: Resolution agreed to in Senate without amendment by Yea-Nay Vote. 51 - 44. Record Vote Number: 517.
  - Recorded vote: Senate session 1, roll 517 (2025-09-15T22:14:53Z)
